pumarix is a vaccine for adults aged 18 years and older against pandemic flu ( influenza ). pandemie flu is characterized by the presence of influenza in 10 million people . pandemian flu is similar to ordinary flu . the vaccine is given to protect against the disease . flu is not a serious condition . all vaccines should be given with pumarx .
pumarix will not be given to you if you have ever had a sudden life - threatening allergic reaction to any of the ingredients of this vaccine ( listed in section 6 ). the active substance is chicken protein , ovalbumin , formaldehyde and sodium deoxycholate . signs of an allergic reaction include itchy skin rash , shortness of breath and swelling of the face or tongue . the vaccine should be given immediately . medical treatment is not recommended if an allergic response has occurred to pumarx . this vaccine is only given to children and adolescents aged 6 years and older . pumaris should not be used if any allergic reaction has occurred . a suspected life  - damaging allergic reaction is not expected to occur . it is recommended that the vaccine is given every 6 weeks .

immunogam belongs to a group of medicines called immunoglobulins ( antibodies ). immunogam is used to treat certain infections in your blood . immunogam can cause increased levels of human hepatitis b immunoglobularins and immunoglobuline g ( igg ). it is used in combination with blood plasma of screened patients . what immunogam does immunogam help to fight hepatis - b virus in haemodialysed patients , who are not vaccinated . it is also used to prevent the spread of hep - 1 infected patients whose body does not produce an immune response . measurable hepathis a antibodies are produced during vaccination . continuous prevention is also recommended for patients who are inf affected by he - 2 .
immunogam may cause an allergic reaction to human immunoglobulins or other blood products . this is called an iga deficiency . an allergic response to iga containing products is rare . children and adolescents ( aged 18 years and over ) who have received immunoglobularins have had adverse reactions such as chills , headache , fever and vomiting . allergic reactions include nausea , arthralgia , joint pain , low blood pressure and moderate low back pain . immunogam is given to children and teenagers with antibodies to hepatitis b immunoglobuin regularly . human hepatis a immunoglobunin injections have been reported in children and teens . if you have a history of a rash , you should tell your doctor .

kinzalmono belongs to a group of medicines called angiotensin ii receptor antagonists . angiostensin is a substance produced in the body that causes blood vessels to narrow , causing your blood pressure to rise . kinzulmono blocks the action of angiodensin in your body , so that the blood vessels relax and your blood temperature is controlled . this helps your body to control your blood tension . the use of kinzalmona is used to treat essential hypertension ( high blood pressure ) in adults . high bloodpressure can damage blood vessels in several organs , leading to heart attack , heart or kidney failure , stroke , blindness .

bexsero is a meningococcal group b vaccine . bexero contains the active substance neisseria mentingitidis group a . the vaccine is used to prevent and treat disease caused by the nasopharyngitiameningitidedis b bacteria . these bacteria cause infections called meningitis , which is inflammation of the brain and spinal cord , and sepsis ( blood poisoning ). the vaccine works by preventing the disease from spreading .
